[30;1m20 | [0m[35m## Installation[0m
[30;1m21 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m22 | [0m[35mInstall the latest version of `universal_pathlib` with pip or conda. Please note[0m
[30;1m23 | [0m[35mthat while this will install `fsspec` as a dependency, for some filesystems, you[0m
